> I'm using 2.4-dist, and this works:
>
> oni:~ $ singularity --version
> 2.4-dist
> oni:~ $ singularity exec --bind /mnt/disk8/genetics/archival/:test_dir:ro
> /mnt/disk2/com/container-images/python2.7.simg python --version
> Python 2.7.14
>

> unicorn:~ $ singularity --version
> 2.4.1-dist

> :ro /mnt/disk2/com/container-images/python2.7.simg python --version

> /: Permission denied

>

> unicorn:~ $ singularity --version
> 2.4.1-dist

>
